# NAME=Protein levels for normal Liver
# DESCRIPTION= data from the Human Protein Atlas - "Normal tissue data". Protein levels are categorized in "High", "Medium", "Low", or "Not detected". It was included all levels of confidence. Color was categorized as -1 (dark red) for "High", -0.66 (medium red) for "Medium", -0.33 (light red) for "Low", and 0 (white) for "Not detected". Only hepatocytes annotated genes were used. 13453 genes included. 22/06/2022.
